	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/script.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'd15dcd6b93803324224c1cbe6c137bfb5c33be1e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd15dcd6b93803324224c1cbe6c137bfb5c33be1e') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd7a200d19547dc4a6ef60b70870fb24de5eca26b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd15dcd6b93803324224c1cbe6c137bfb5c33be1e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus_base.js');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('oidplus_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') != '759847f0cfa4b7bda048ab37e8a8850046f42536') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') !== '759847f0cfa4b7bda048ab37e8a8850046f42536') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') !== '1cfc4994495898879ca8043215c533f5477307f1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') !== '759847f0cfa4b7bda048ab37e8a8850046f42536') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '4555fffeebbc7d77ca662a6e1123316b98affc0f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '4555fffeebbc7d77ca662a6e1123316b98affc0f') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'bf08db0f32b46cf2da1e2affc73639c3ade3dc86') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '4555fffeebbc7d77ca662a6e1123316b98affc0f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') != '6e182c2450e7424f7d7148be9f463aad80a6e23b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== '6e182c2450e7424f7d7148be9f463aad80a6e23b') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== 'f26540dc20301ae8743deda795534bedf3afb75e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== '6e182c2450e7424f7d7148be9f463aad80a6e23b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 385\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 385') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
